Everything that is outside the reach of decadent megacorporations is run by warlords, upstart rulers, and crazed individuals. It's what we were afraid of - we caught the attention of some bigger fish. Luckily for us, they are still unaware of the treasure we hold, so we are targeted like a casual warband, one of many. The bigger problem is that we were noticed by the biggest and the strongest group in the vicinity - League of Women is a paramilitary organization that boasts that they are direct descendants of a rightful government and military from beyond the fall. Given their skills, armaments, discipline, and hierarchy - that might not be so far from the truth. \n\nWorse is, they are particularly focused on acquiring as many males as possible - due to their "No Males Allowed" all males are to be forcibly acquired whenever possible and used to pump their semen out to produce more soldiers for the League - with a distinct possibility of producing new males for their war efforts. For now, it was successful at prolonging the inevitable and giving them an upper hand when fighting other groups.\n\nPart of League motivational speech, recovered from an abandoned outpost:\n"We, the Womankind, are the only descendant of humanity! \nMales were among the rulers before, but they doomed us all!\nNow, it's only fair if they will SERVE US in our task of restoring what is rightfully ours!\nFor the League! For the Womankind! For the World!"=这就是我们所害怕的——我们引起了一些更大的鱼的注意。\n对我们来说幸运的是，他们仍然不知道我们拥有的宝藏，所以我们就像休闲战队一样成为目标，只是众多战队之一。\n更大的问题是，我们被附近最大、最强的团体注意到了——妇女联盟是一个准军事组织，自称是堕落后合法政府和军队的直系后裔。\n考虑到他们的技能、武器、纪律和等级制度——这可能与事实相差不远。\n\n\n更糟糕的是，他们特别注重获取尽可能多的男性——由于他们的“不允许男性”，只要有可能，所有男性都会被强行获取，并用来抽出精液，为联盟生产更多的士兵——很可能为他们的战争努力生产新的男性。\n就目前而言，它成功地延长了不可避免的时间，并让他们在与其他团体战斗时占据了上风。\n\n\n联盟励志演讲的一部分，从废弃的前哨基地回收：\n“我们，女性，是人类唯一的后裔！\n男性曾经是统治者，但他们注定了我们所有人！\n\n现在，如果他们愿意为我们服务，帮助我们恢复属于我们的东西，那才是公平的！\n\n为了联盟！\n为了女性！\n为了世界！”

Post-Romanticism=后浪漫主义
Hello Jane, I'm here.=你好，简，我在这里。
I assume there's a "but" following?=我猜后面应该有一个“但是”吧？
<b><style\=ColorGreen>Ashley:</style></b> Of course! Tell me!=<b><style\=ColorGreen>阿什利：</style></b> 当然！\n告诉我！
<b><style\=ColorGreen>Ashley:</style></b> Well, luckily... I am <i>very</i> slippery...~=<b><style\=ColorGreen>阿什利：</style></b> 嗯，幸运的是……我是 <i>非常</i> 滑...~
<b><style\=ColorGreen>Ashley:</style></b> Just going to say ahead of time, I don't want you to think I'm actively looking for problems or faults, because I'm not!=<b><style\=ColorGreen>阿什利：</style></b> 只是提前说一下，我不想让你认为我在积极寻找问题或错误，因为我不是！

<b><style\=ColorGreen>Ashley:</style></b> *giggle* Well, it hasn't happened yet, so I wouldn't know.=<b><style\=ColorGreen>阿什利：</style></b> *咯咯*好吧，这还没有发生，所以我不知道。
And what if you're caught?=如果你被抓住了怎么办？
<b><style\=ColorGreen>Ashley:</style></b> And when the time finally comes... you slip through your carefully crafted route and go for it...!=<b><style\=ColorGreen>阿什利：</style></b> 当时机最终到来时...您将滑过精心设计的路线并奋力前行...！
<b><style\=ColorGreen>Ashley:</style></b> The important thing is to be patient and not jump at all opportunities. Leaving distractions, maybe even hints is also a good idea.=<b><style\=ColorGreen>阿什利：</style></b> 重要的是要有耐心，不要抓住所有机会。\n留下干扰，甚至暗示也是个好主意。
